### 2. @Jackson-fh7uv (2045 chars)

> Trying just means not giving up so if you try you canâ€™t lose and if you have nothing you have nothing to lose so just try I know there will always be bigger and harder problems but each time you solve one you get a little bit better cause the ultimate output of each problem solved isnâ€™t that you solved the problem itâ€™s you Pain is like the ground it will always be there sure you can take a plane to avoid it but you will always return to the ground there is no avoiding it pains the same way, like you can try to avoid it with drugs or scrolling or porn or whatever you want, but it's always gonna be there. So I think if you say pain is a bad thing, then you set yourself up to be unhappy forever, because you can never avoid it. Like pain is there. But the ground is not a bad thing. For sure. The ground is just proof that you're on Earth, and without it, you never learn how to walk. And pain, it is just proof that you're alive and And I think you need to let yourself feel the pain, because as much as we want to have these healthy, positive motivations, at least for me, it's a lot more effective to run from the pain. But just because you run from it doesn't mean it's bad. All that means is that it's something that makes you run. And here's the thing You don't need to know what you're running towards. All you need to know is what you don't want, and then you can run as fast as you can in the other direction. Because if the thing you're running from is wanting to end your own life like it's that bad, that death is a viable option, no amount of suffering or discomfort is gonna be worse than that, right? So just pick something, it doesn't even matter what, and just put the pain towards that. Because, you know, you're gonna suck in the beginning because you don't know what you're doing and you're new. But if you do something for enough time, enough times, you will become good at it. And if you're good at something, it's a hell of a lot easier to enjoy it. So that's how I see it. A very wise man named reid olson said this

### 12. @jimmiizzy6283 (1475 chars)

> @Alex-Kuzma
Are you holding your guitar? Do you have the chords yet? Can you play the song? Ear it out, just like Rick taught you. 
Don't read my chords, until you give it a try, then I'll give them to you (after listening to the song 1 time through and learning it in real time, so there its a basic interpretation, I'm a basic guy)
Intro: Em, D    (12 fret bar the top 3 strings for Em, then drop down to D major 11, 10,10.  Pick them straight and down in triplets, and to nail the timing quickly, just play the lowest note only right on the quarter note. Once you do that, you'll have it.)
Chorus: Em, walk up to G major (E, F#, G), then keep walking, (A, Bm, then back down to 'A', then back down 'F#, E'.) It's a really walking part, so just keep walking up to the next chord, then back down, then all the way back down through F# back to Em.   The song is in Em so it's always, Em, G major, A major, Bm. 
It's also really fun to, on the very first low note introduction to reach down and pluck your open low E string with the piano, and then pluck the open D string when you switch to the D chord. It messed my timing up, but if you nail it, it would be real good.
That's about all I know, as I only listened to it once.
Great song, gave me goosebumps after listening to the back story. And the girl was so pretty, the low end was so thick and rich, the singing very syncopated (try playing and singing it, if you do that, you're doing real good.), I really enjoyed it.

### 9. @sadhentaihours4122 (2058 chars)

> My uncle's Grandfather (èˆ…çˆ·çˆ·)died in a motorcycle accident a few days ago, a few days before Chinese New Year.
And my mother's side of Grandma died in peace last year, also a few days before Chinese New Year.
They both are a big part of my life, and are just gone in just a second. I was outside of town, can't even make it to the hospital.
As a Chinese, especially in my 30s, most of us are already out of our hometown, Swatow/Shantou(æ±•å¤´), to make it out for a living in the big cities like Guangzhou or Shenzhen. While I was living in Xiamen, struggling to keep myself alive, I still miss the food, the scenery, the memories, the parents, and the homies in Swatow.
Every time I heard this song, even I don't know any Spanish(Shout out to all the local translators), but I can hear the loneliness, sadness, and also the "i got u homie" vibes.
It also brings me a message: You gotta do something when it's not too late.
So I did.
When I get back to my hometown, bumping this song repeatedly, I immediately tryin' my best to speak Teochew dialect every single time when I have the opportunity to talk to someone, even my first language is Mandarin. And taking loads of photos of everything: The family, the scenery, the locals, the homies.
Last night I was in a car with my family, I posted all the photos on my local social media, and a screenshot of the"DebÃ­ tirar mÃ¡s fotos de cuando te tuve
DebÃ­ darte mÃ¡s besos y abrazo' las veces que pude"line with Chinese Translations of it.

Today is the first day of the Chinese New Year, the Year of the Horse. I hope you can keep rocking and doing your best. I hope everything you dreamed will be succeed, and also, when the time is right, take more photos, call or meet often with your family, your homies, please!

### 11. @ekawixrots (990 chars)

> what the description says in english

From the full and the bomb to the reggaeton

(1500s-1990s)

In the mid-nineteenth century, the musical genre of dance emerged, created in the city of Ponce and influenced by the European tradition.

La borinqueÃ±a, the song that will later become the anthem of Puerto Rico, was composed as a dance in 1867. The following year the poet Lola Rodriguez de TiÃ³ wrote the lyrics to what is known today as "The Revolutionary BorinqueÃ±a."

The lyrics were an ode and a call to arms in the struggle for the independence of Puerto Rico. These lyrics were written in the revolutionary context of the Grito de Lares, an independence insurrection that took place on September 23, 1868.

At the beginning of the next century, in 1903, Manuel FernÃ¡ndez Juncos rewrote the lyrics of the song where he alluded to the discovery of Puerto Rico and its natural beauty.

This will be the version that the government of Puerto Rico will adopt as the official anthem in 1952.

### 17. @siskskva (757 chars)

> "DtMF" is a nostalgic reflection on the importance of treasuring moments with loved ones. Bad Bunny expresses regret for not capturing more photographs during meaningful experiences, emphasizing how those memories become valuable over time. The song invites us to value the present and the people around us, reminding us of the transience of life and the relevance of preserving memories.
Bad Bunny has sparked speculation about his relationship with his ex-girlfriend, Gabriela Berlingeri. Some fans interpret the lyrics as reflecting nostalgia and regret for not having captured more moments during his relationship with her. Lines like "I should have taken more photos, kissed more, hugged more" suggest a desire to have treasured more memories together.

### 9. @aureliesoulard-amann5875 (1170 chars)

> As my name doesn't indicate, I was born in Korea and was adopted. I always felt like I had to explain everything to others: my parents are not like me but French; the country where I was born is somewhere between China and Japan. I am now 49 years old, and it has been 2 years (only) that I have been reviving my Korean roots, fully embracing Korean culture and proudly wearing (especially through modern hanboks) this identity that I ignored so much out of a desire to integrate and which nevertheless gives me so much energy today: that of childhood where one is so curious, daring and ambitious. I received the song "Golden" as a new healing treatment for my flaw, my wound. The more I listen to it, the more it moves me. I also consider it as a confirmation of what I have secretly wished for since my middle school years: I can make my place by assuming who I am entirely and do great things in this world, not only for my family and loved ones, but also for the people with whom I may be in contact, or who may be touched (not by my vocal performances!) by the gestures or words I could address to them. That would give so much meaning to my coming into the world!

You cant be not into kpop, not if you like pop, rnb, electronic, hip hop, etc etc. Because its literally just those musical styles and more in Korean but with more of a focus on intricate choreography and a visual stage presentation compared to Western standards. ### 22. @Starbreed (718 chars)

> Every once in a while, my sister and I will take turns and pick a random movie (purposely one we'd never watch ourselves) on Netflix and see how long we can watch it before turning it off. 

I picked K-Pop Demon Hunters. We cringed together. We laughed together. I know I had tears in my eyes at multiple points. But I dont know about her, because I couldn't look away from the tv. And as soon as it was over, I turned to my sister and almost asked her "do you want to watch that again?"

But instead we just sort of sat there in stunned silence. It was such a deep and surprisingly human story, and it was such a shock to both of us how we never even touched the remote except to turn up the volume. Incredible movie.

### 24. @korea-sky (673 chars)

> If a passerby hears this song, they might say it's just another K-pop song, but if you find out what the movie is about, you'll be in tears. The story of Rumi overcoming the fact that she's half-human, half-demon and mustering up the courage to defeat the devil that she can't reveal to the world is actually intertwined with the struggles of the singer EJAE, who sang this song, during her unknown days as a trainee, and the fact that she's finally becoming known to the world through this song is what makes the song even more poignant and profound. That's why the emotion you feel while watching the movie is a mixture of inexplicable emotions and tears that come later.

### 1. @Crystalartchive_7 (1010 chars)

> found out how to stream bts songs on youtube from a video so i thought to share it, for peoples who don't know how to stream :

1. Use search bar - Always search for the MV manually. Don't click on links!

2. Watch the FULL MV - Don't skip or fast-forward.

3. Watch in 480p or higher with sound ON.

4. Log in to your account - Views only count when you're signed in.

5. Watch different videos in between - Avoid looping just one video. Watch other BTS content or take breaks.

6. Like, comment, and share! Engagement boosts visibility.

what we SHOULDN'T DO

1. DON'T mute the video. (Use low volume instead)

2. DON'T use incognito mode.

3. DON'T refresh or replay continuously. It may not count as a new view.

4. DON'T skip ads. If you can, let them play.

5. DON'T run multiple tabs or devices at once with the same account. 

BONUS :
1) Use multiple devices/accounts if you can

2) Clear watch history or log out and in after a few hours

3) Use playlists smartly: mix MVs, live stages, and interviews

### 7. @DipaliNagdeve-x1x (723 chars)

> How to Stream on YouTube:
1. Create a YouTube account
2. Search for a BTS jin  song 
3. Watch the song without skipping
4. Turn off Autoplay
5. Keep the volume above 50% during streaming (Streaming won't work on low volume...use headphones, it's better)
6. Video quality should be 480p (Low-quality videos aren't streamed)
7. When the video is half played, like it and leave a nice comment (Don't use emojis in comments)
8. Don't play the same song back-to-back
9. Don't stream offline/VPN songs
10. Don't stream continuously, take breaks. Stream a playlist, then search for the song, play another playlist, take a break, and repeat the process (Playlist â†’ Search â†’ Another playlist â†’ Break â†’ Repeat). You're done streaming

### 7. @Liamm06 (1816 chars)

> Claro, aquÃ­ tienes las definiciones de cada tÃ©rmino relacionadas con la cocina y los alimentos:

1. *Higiene:* Conjunto de normas y prÃ¡cticas que se aplican para mantener la limpieza y evitar contaminaciones en los alimentos, utensilios, superficies y personal, con el fin de garantizar la seguridad alimentaria.

2. *Textura:* CaracterÃ­stica fÃ­sica de un alimento que se percibe al tacto o al masticar, como si es crujiente, suave, fibroso, duro o cremoso.

3. *Consistencia:* Grado de densidad, firmeza o espesor que presenta un alimento, ya sea lÃ­quido, semisÃ³lido o sÃ³lido. Por ejemplo, una sopa puede tener una consistencia ligera o espesa.

4. *Hervido:* TÃ©cnica de cocciÃ³n en la que los alimentos se cocinan en agua u otro lÃ­quido que ha alcanzado los 100 Â°C, provocando burbujas constantes en la superficie.

5. *Apariencia:* Aspecto visual de un alimento, incluyendo su color, forma y presentaciÃ³n. Es uno de los primeros factores que influye en la aceptaciÃ³n del plato.

### 3. @TD55_00 (2208 chars)

> The song opens with a soft, melodic introduction that sets a contemplative mood. 

The first verse introduces the idea of shedding layers, both literally and metaphorically. 

The lyrics suggest a desire to be seen for who one truly is, beyond the facades that people often present to the world. 

This theme of vulnerability is a recurring motif throughout the song, as the narrator expresses a longing for genuine connection.


As the chorus hits, the repetition of the phrase "undressed" emphasizes the act of revealing oneself, not just physically but emotionally. 

This moment serves as a powerful declaration of the narrator's willingness to be open and honest, inviting the listener to consider their own experiences with intimacy. 

The use of vivid imagery in the lyrics paints a picture of a relationship where both parties are encouraged to let go of their insecurities and embrace their true selves.
In the second verse, the song delves deeper into the complexities of love and attraction. 

The lyrics reflect on the push and pull of desire, highlighting the tension that often exists in romantic relationships. 

The narrator grapples with feelings of fear and excitement, illustrating the duality of wanting to be close to someone while also fearing the potential for heartbreak. 

This internal conflict resonates with many listeners, as it captures the essence of modern love.
The bridge of the song introduces a moment of introspection, where the narrator questions their own motivations and desires. 

This section adds depth to the narrative, as it reveals the struggle between wanting to be vulnerable and the fear of being hurt. 

The lyrics here are poignant, showcasing Sombr's ability to articulate complex emotions in a relatable way.
As the song progresses towards its conclusion, the repetition of the chorus reinforces the central theme of vulnerability. 

The final lines echo a sense of acceptance, suggesting that while being "undressed" can be daunting, it is also a necessary step towards forming meaningful connections. 

The song ends on a reflective note, leaving listeners with a sense of hope and the understanding that true intimacy requires courage and authenticity.

### 14. @bruzote (931 chars)

> @aei aei - Oh, please, just try having a genuine and true thought. Nobody is being victimized here. It's a musical story of someone who wishes he could see her and his eyes in kids they had together. But that lyric doesn't hurt. The character is trying to avoid pain, so the lyrics have to flip what he wants to have to what he doesn't want. That's Story Writing 101. And the sensible contrapositive of that is NOT wanting to see someone else's eyes in her kids. So, for crissake, grow up! You sound like a young adult whose pathetically-limited mind heard a novel idea of "toxic masculinuty" and now thinks the whole world must be seen through that lens, like people who learn about Freud and then think everything is about sex. One day, even without trying, you're going to grow bored - even sick and tired - of your overwrought, self-righteous anger. For the rest of us hearing the likes of you, that day can't come soon enough.

### 4. @Nothingseen (1160 chars)

> I've been doin' some thankin' about why this song hits so hard, and I think there's a subtle redefinition in it that is desperately needed but isn't ever asked for. The man she needs is one who can and will talk to her. She doesn't praise boldness here, but instead connection and communication. She wants to meet his best friend, she wonders where he is; this isn't about someone who's pushing in to talk to her, but instead someone who follows her invitation.
This is a redefinition of what is desirable. She doesn't talk about appearance or prowess or power in any way, but instead the ability to communicate. It's an intimate and gentle invitation to become close through words, because she wants that and that's what the man she needs will do.
Which is also a redefinition of desirable masculinity. The Man doesn't take her, he talks to her. She literally says be the man man man man here and it's really hard to miss it.
The reason it feels so warm isn't just because of how its musically crafted, although that's a big part of it for sure. I think it's also using female agency to define desirability in a way that's kind, good, and inherently intimate.

ğŸ‘ 6 Â· 5 days ago

### 12. @Liamm06 (1816 chars)

> Claro, aquÃ­ tienes las definiciones de cada tÃ©rmino relacionadas con la cocina y los alimentos:

1. *Higiene:* Conjunto de normas y prÃ¡cticas que se aplican para mantener la limpieza y evitar contaminaciones en los alimentos, utensilios, superficies y personal, con el fin de garantizar la seguridad alimentaria.

2. *Textura:* CaracterÃ­stica fÃ­sica de un alimento que se percibe al tacto o al masticar, como si es crujiente, suave, fibroso, duro o cremoso.

3. *Consistencia:* Grado de densidad, firmeza o espesor que presenta un alimento, ya sea lÃ­quido, semisÃ³lido o sÃ³lido. Por ejemplo, una sopa puede tener una consistencia ligera o espesa.

4. *Hervido:* TÃ©cnica de cocciÃ³n en la que los alimentos se cocinan en agua u otro lÃ­quido que ha alcanzado los 100 Â°C, provocando burbujas constantes en la superficie.

5. *Apariencia:* Aspecto visual de un alimento, incluyendo su color, forma y presentaciÃ³n. Es uno de los primeros factores que influye en la aceptaciÃ³n del plato.

6. *Sabor:* SensaciÃ³n que percibimos al comer, resultado de la combinaciÃ³n de los cinco gustos bÃ¡sicos (dulce, salado, Ã¡cido, amargo y umami) junto con el aroma y la textura del alimento.

7. *TÃ©cnicas en cocina:* MÃ©todos o procedimientos usados para preparar, cocinar y presentar alimentos, como asar, freÃ­r, cocer al vapor, hornear, entre otros.

8. *Seguridad en cocina:* Conjunto de normas y precauciones destinadas a prevenir accidentes, quemaduras, cortes y otros riesgos durante el trabajo en la cocina, asÃ­ como a evitar la contaminaciÃ³n alimentaria.

9. *OrganizaciÃ³n del trabajo:* PlanificaciÃ³n y distribuciÃ³n eficiente de tareas, tiempos, herramientas y espacios en la cocina para asegurar una preparaciÃ³n ordenada, limpia y efectiva de los alimentos.

### 13. @jess.singswithleaves6 (809 chars)

> For the non-Spanish speakers, here's the history lesson he included on the"slide"!

Porto Rico: The Early Years of Americanization in Puerto Rico (1898-1936)

Puerto Rico has had different names throughout its history. Indigenous communities called it Burunquen or BorikÃ©n. Upon their arrival, the Spanish renamed it the Island of San Juan Bautista. Later, it became known as the Island of Puerto Rico until it was simply called Puerto Rico.

At the beginning of the 20th century (1900s), just five years after the American invasion, its name was changed again. Puerto Rico became known as "Porto Rico" in official U.S. documents. This name change was due to the fact that Americans were unable to pronounce the word "Puerto." The new name lasted a couple of decades before it was changed back to Puerto Rico.

### 2. @Winterbear.08 (1270 chars)

> The blue rose is a fascinating symbol, largely because it doesn't naturally occur. This fact has heavily influenced its meaning. Here's a breakdown of the blue rose's symbolism:
 * The Unattainable:
   * Because blue roses were historically difficult to create, they've come to represent things that are out of reach, impossible, or highly desired but difficult to achieve.
   * This can include dreams, hopes, and desires that seem beyond grasp.
 * Mystery and Intrigue:
   * The rare and somewhat unnatural appearance of a blue rose lends it an air of mystery and intrigue.
   * It can symbolize the unknown, the enigmatic, and the desire to explore the unseen.
 * The Impossible Dream:
   * Blue roses are often associated with the pursuit of the impossible dream, the striving for something that may seem out of reach.
 * Unique and Extraordinary:
   * Their rarity makes them a symbol of uniqueness and extraordinary beauty.
 * New Beginnings:
   * In some interpretations, especially with the advancement of genetic modification that has made blue roses more available, they can also symbolize new possibilities, and pushing past limitations.
Essentially, the blue rose captures the essence of longing for something special, something that transcends the ordinary.
